@tab 关于我
![](https://s3.amazonaws.com/static2.postcrossing.com/avatars/140x140/ecjsc6b4jdqmo83xjk6293882b42f86f.jpg)

:::info 个人简介

Hello, my name is Arthur, I recently developed a passion for cycling, and my goal is to complete 100 rides of 100 kilometers each. I’m currently at 22 out of 100!(update on 2025/12/21)My avatar is my daughter, who just turned 3 years old. Her nickname is Xiaoxiao(笑笑). She just started kindergarten in September 2025. Isn’t she adorable?If you’re looking for postcard ideas to send me, here are a few suggestions:
- any postcards and stamps with themes related to cycling, running, and other sports！
- you can recommend any famous local coffee bean brands, I’d love to hear about them!
- Xiaoxiao loves animals, so any cute animal postcards would be highly appreciated!
- Postcards featuring doctors or local TV series recommendations would be wonderful.
- I would be thrilled to receive postcards written in the language of your country (e.g., greeting words for my family).
- Series relating to special festivals in your country.
- Beautiful landscapes from your city or country.
- Any other postcard you choose!If you’ve sent me a postcard a long time ago and it hasn’t been registered, please let me know. My email is fsyflh@gmail.com, and I’ll check my mailbox promptly.I recommend printing out the Chinese address and pasting it on the postcard, as it helps increase delivery efficiency.来自港澳台的朋友/海外华侨们，欢迎写中文寄过来！非常期待你们写的汉字！

## 二.地图展示

:::tip 地图颜色
紫色：收发均有的国家
绿色：仅有收/仅有发的国家
灰色：收发均无的国家
:::

:::echarts

```js
const data = await fetch(
  "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator/main/output/calendar.json"
).then((res) => res.json());

const date = new Date();
const year = date.getFullYear().toString().padStart(4, "0");

const option = {
  tooltip: {},
  visualMap: {
    show: false,
    min: 1,
```

### 收发记录（月度）

:::echarts

```js
const data = await fetch(
  "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator/main/output/month.json"
).then((res) => res.json());

var date = data.map(function (item) {
  return item.date;
});

var sent = data.map(function (item) {
  return item.sent;
});

var sentSum = sent.reduce(function (acc, curr) {
  return acc + curr;
}, 0);

var received = data.map(function (item) {
  return item.received;
});

var receivedSum = received.reduce(function (acc, curr) {
  return acc + curr;
}, 0);

sentName = sentSum + "张已寄出";
receivedName = receivedSum + "张已收到";

const option = {
  title: {
    text: "",
    left: "center",
  },
  legend: {
    data: [sentName, receivedName],
  },
  tooltip: {
    trigger: "axis",
  },
  xAxis: {
    type: "category",
    data: date,
  },
  yAxis: {
    type: "value",
  },
  dataZoom: [
    {
      start: 0,
    },
    {
      type: "inside",
    },
  ],
  series: [
    {
      name: sentName,
      data: sent,
      type: "line",
      smooth: true,
    },
    {
      name: receivedName,
      data: received,
      type: "line",
      smooth: true,
    },
  ],
};
```

:::

### 数据统计

:::tabs
@tab 国家分布

::: echarts

```js
const data = await fetch(
  "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator/main/output/stats.json"
).then((res) => res.json());

const option = {
  title: {
    text: "",
    subtext: "",
    left: "center",
  },
  tooltip: {
    trigger: "item",
    formatter: "{b} : {c}",
  },
  xAxis: {
    type: "category",
    data: data.map(item => item.name), // 假设数据项有name属性
  },
  yAxis: {
    type: "value",
  },
  dataZoom: [{end:60}],
  series: [
    {
      name: "",
      type: "bar", // 修改为柱状图
      data: data.map(item => item.value), // 假设数据项有value属性
      emphasis: {
        itemStyle: {
          shadowBlur: 10,
          shadowOffsetX: 0,
          shadowColor: "rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5)",
        },
      },
      label: {
        show: true,
        position: "top",
      },
    },
  ],
}
;
```

@tab 内容
* 卡片文字

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 识别]`
Warm greetings from cold Belarus!
My name is Karina, I'm 27 y.o. Immediately after graduating from university, where I studied law, I started working at the investigative committee. I worked there for 2 years and resigned because it was morally difficult job, but sometimes it was interesting. Most often, I investigated thefts of property or money stolen from bank cards through online fraud. Once a week, we were on duty, responding to reports of crimes that had been reported to the police.
Now I work at the transport inspectorate, where I monitor compliance with taxi regulations. I have much less work here than before, so in my spare time I sign postcards at my job.
The postcard shows holidays and rituals of Belarusians and our national costumes
Best wishes for you and your family,
Karina 😊

* 翻译：

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 翻译]`
来自寒冷白俄罗斯的亲切问候！
我叫Karina，今年27岁。大学主修法律，毕业后我立即进入调查委员会工作。我在那里工作了两年，后来因为这份工作在道德上让人感到沉重而辞职了，但有时它也挺有趣的。我处理得最多的是财产盗窃案，或是通过网络诈骗从银行卡中窃取钱财的案件。我们每周有一次值班，负责响应向警方报案的犯罪事件。
现在我在交通监察部门工作，负责监督出租车行业的合规情况。这里的工作比以前轻松多了，所以我在空闲时间会写写明信片。
这张明信片展示了白俄罗斯人的节日、习俗以及我们的民族服装。
祝你和你的家人一切顺利，
Karina 😊


:::

> Hello Siyuan!! Greetings from Japan.
I live in Yokohama, next to Tokyo.
中国の漢字は難しいです。日本の小学校では1026文字も習います。
When writing an address in Japan, we write '様' at the end of the name, but do we do it in China? 元気 でね!
♡ Xiaoxiao かわいいね ♡
Azusa"

* 翻译：

> 你好，思远！！来自日本的问候。
我住在横滨，靠近东京。
中国的汉字好难啊。在日本的小学学习多达1026个汉字。
在日本写地址时，我们会在名字后加上“様”（先生/女士的敬称），但在中国也会这样吗？祝你健康愉快！
♡ 笑笑，好可爱呀 ♡
梓


@tab 额外消息
* 消息原文

> Thank you for your message. Yes, that's right. Kanji is difficult, but English is difficult too. Sorry for writing in Japanese. I always use Google Translate. Take care. Happy Postcrossing. Azusa

* 翻译：

> 感谢你的留言。是的，没错。汉字很难，但英语也难。抱歉用日语写。我总是使用谷歌翻译。保重。祝你快乐的明信片交换。梓玲

:::

> 📤 [Bosnia-Herzegovina](https://www.bing.com/maps/?cp=43.84864~18.35644&lvl=12.0&setlang=zh-Hans) 2024/06/20 10:10 (当地)

 📏 8,740 | ⏱ 113

:::tabs
@tab 图片
<div class="image-preview">  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/gallery/picture/vf7n495616r3oie9uad7lx4lurt4pkut.jpg" />  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/template/content/BA-14379.webp" /></div>

@tab 内容
* 卡片文字

> Hello Feng,
my name is Leila and I am thrilled to introduce you to Bosnia, an ex-Yugoslavian country in the heart of the Balkans.
I'll start with "Ćejf", a concept about savoring the moment, like enjoying a cup of coffee or a conversation with a friend, taking time to relax is a cherished tradition here.
Jufat - a Bosnian treat, a kind of stubborn pride or defiance. It helped Bosnians persevere through challenging times.
Deret - it conveys a deep sense of sorrow and heartache, it reflects pain, but also embodies the idea of enduring and sharing one's burden with others.     
Veliki pozdrav iz Sarajeva

* 翻译：

> 你好，冯，
我叫Leila，我很高兴向你介绍波斯尼亚，这个位于巴尔干半岛中心的前南斯拉夫国家。
我从“Ćejf”开始，这是关于享受当下的概念，比如享受一杯咖啡或与朋友的谈话，放松时间在这里是珍贵的传统。
Jufat - 一种波斯尼亚的美食，一种倔强的骄傲或反抗。它帮助波斯尼亚人在困难时期坚持下去。
Deret - 传达深刻的悲伤和心痛，反映痛苦，同时也体现了忍耐和与他人分享重担的理念。
来自萨拉热窝的诚挚问候

 📏 7,699 | ⏱ 15

:::tabs
@tab 图片
<div class="image-preview">  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/gallery/picture/4ttbpxkkr9v2qr10jxkkaj3wqof97sdz.jpg" />  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/template/content/FI-4633650.webp" /></div>

@tab 内容
* 卡片文字

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 识别]`
Hei, 17th of Juney 2024. Greeting from sunny Finland. Now at 8.30 am is 20 C. Sun has arisen at 3.37 am and will go down at 10.50 pm. I'm a biology, geography, and social studies teacher (also math this school year) in upper comprehensive school for pupils with 13-16 years old. I like my job very much. I have MCTD. It's rare of rheumatism disease. I have so much pain in articulations that handwriting isn't possible. June 2023, I got another rheumatism diagnoses, psoriatic arthritis. I try to be positive. I have personal assistant who help me with Postcrossing and many other things. On school time I got to work by taxi because public transport isn't going near to school (I should walk from bus stop about a one km). At school I'm not allowed to walk stairs alone, my classroom is at 3rd floor and in my school isn't lift/elevator. I want to go work because when I'm teaching, I don't think about pain. I have use wheelchair in my free time. Our school year ended at 1st of June and back to schools we go at mid-August. Anne (veverka)

* 翻译：

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 翻译]`
Hei（芬兰语：你好），2024年6月17日。来自阳光明媚的芬兰的问候。现在是早上8点30分，气温20摄氏度。太阳在凌晨3点37分升起，将于晚上10点50分落下。我是一名生物、地理和社会研究老师（本学年也教数学），在面向13至16岁学生的初中高年级任教。我非常喜欢我的工作。

我患有MCTD（混合性结缔组织病），这是一种罕见的风湿病。我的关节疼痛非常严重，以至于无法手写。2023年6月，我被诊断出患有另一种风湿病——银屑病关节炎。我努力保持积极乐观。我有一位私人助理，她会协助我进行Postcrossing（明信片交换）以及处理其他许多事情。

上学期间，我乘出租车去上班，因为公共交通工具不到学校附近（我需要从公交车站步行约一公里）。在学校里，我不被允许独自走楼梯，我的教室在三楼，而且学校里没有电梯。我想去工作，因为当我教学时，我就不会去想疼痛的事了。我在空闲时间会使用轮椅。

我们的学年在6月1日结束，我们将于8月中旬重返校园。

Anne (veverka)


:::

[IN-592435](https://www.postcrossing.com/postcards/IN-592435)

> 来自 *用户已注销* 🇮🇳

:::tabs
@tab 图片
<div class="image-preview">  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/gallery/picture/" />  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/template/content/IN-592435.webp" /></div>

@tab 内容
* 卡片文字

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 识别]`
7 May 2024
Bengaluru
Dear, 
Feng Siyuan
Namaskara from karnataka India,
I'm thrilled to share with you a unique aspect of our cultural heritage
Bhuta kola, a traditional folk dance form that's an integral
Part of our state's rich traditions.
Bhuta kola is a vibrant and energetic dance form that's performed to appease the spirits and ancestors. The dancers, adorned in elaborate costumes and masks, enact mythological stories and legends, accompanied by rhythmic drumbeats and music. This ancient art form is a testament to our state's cultural diversity and rich history.
Thank you!

* 翻译：

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 翻译]`
2024年5月7日
班加罗尔
亲爱的冯思远：
来自印度卡纳塔克邦的问候（Namaskara），
很高兴能与你分享我们文化遗产中独特的一面——“布塔科拉”（Bhuta kola），这是一种传统的民间舞蹈形式，也是我们邦丰富传统中不可或缺的一部分。
“布塔科拉”是一种充满活力和能量的舞蹈，旨在安抚神灵和祖先。舞者们身着精致的服装，戴着面具，在节奏感十足的鼓点和音乐伴奏下，演绎着神话故事和传说。这种古老的艺术形式是我们邦文化多样性和悠久历史的见证。
谢谢！


:::

:::tabs
@tab 图片
<div class="image-preview">  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/gallery/picture/c6j8qns0fwqmo1bi5zinj0rjk87oyxsa.jpg" />  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/template/content/US-10240079.webp" /></div>

@tab 内容
* 卡片文字

> Stamp Out Boring Mail!
14 march 2024
Hello from Minnesota. We are called "The Land of 10000 Lakes" and "The North Star State". 
Your daughter is super cute!
I've lived here most of my life, but also in other states. I like it here but winters are cold.
Wishing you and your family health and joy, Melissa.

* 翻译：

> 消灭无聊的邮件！
2024 年 3 月 14 日
你好，来自明尼苏达州。 我们被称为“万湖之地”和“北极星之州”。
你女儿超级可爱！
我一生大部分时间都住在这里，但也在其他州住过。 我喜欢这里，但冬天很冷。
祝您和您的家人健康快乐，梅丽莎。


@tab 额外消息
* 消息原文

> “Hello! I'm glad you liked the card and stamps. Yes, some of the stamps that I use are very old. Some are more than 50 or 60 years old, and some 1-cent stamps that I use are even more than 100 years old! Our postal service allows us to keep using them. I had never heard of the Tomb Sweeping holiday, so I looked it up online and read about it. It sounds like a wonderful way to honor lost loved ones and ancestors. I hope you found it peaceful and heart-filling. Sending best wishes on a sunny Saturday in Minnesota! Melissa”

* 翻译：

> “你好！ 我很高兴你喜欢这张卡片和邮票。 是的，我使用的一些邮票非常旧。 有些已经有50或60多年的历史了，有些我使用的1美分邮票甚至有100多年的历史了！ 我们的邮政服务使我们能够继续使用它们。 我从来没有听说过清明节，所以我在网上查了一下并了解了它。 这听起来是一种纪念逝去亲人和祖先的绝妙方式。 我希望你发现它平静且充满心灵。 在明尼苏达州阳光明媚的星期六送上最美好的祝福！ 梅丽莎”

:::

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 识别]`
March 01, 2024, 7°C, rainy

Hello Arthur and your family,

I'm delighted to be sending you a postcard. I'm Lara and I'm from Stuttgart, Germany.
Today is my friend's birthday. He's turning 41. However, he doesn't enjoy celebrating his birthday much, so we're working as usual today and will go out for dinner after work. My friend is from South Korea, and we both love Korean food. Normally, we enjoy cooking ourselves, but in the past few months, many Korean restaurants have opened here, and some of them are quite good. :)
Last year, we also spent a month in South Korea with his family. It was one of the best trips I've ever taken. I learned so much about the culture and life there, as we stayed with his family, of course. I'm already looking forward to the next time we visit his family.

At the front of the card in German it says: Speak kindly to everyone, everything you say should be seasoned with salt. Endeavor to find the right words for each person. ♡ Lara

* 翻译：

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 翻译]`
2024年3月1日，7℃，雨天

你好，Arthur和你的家人们，

很高兴能给你们寄这张明信片。我是Lara，来自德国斯图加特。
今天是我的朋友的生日，他41岁了。但他不太喜欢大张旗鼓地庆祝生日，所以我们今天照常工作，下班后会出去吃顿晚餐。我的朋友来自韩国，我们俩都很爱吃韩餐。通常我们喜欢自己做饭，但过去几个月里，这里开了好多家韩国餐厅，有些味道还真不错。:)
去年，我们还和他家人在韩国待了一个月。那是我去过最棒的旅行之一。我在那里学到了很多关于当地文化和生活的知识，当然，因为我们是和他家人住在一起的。我已经开始期待下一次去探望他的家人了。

卡片正面用德语写着：待人友善，言语要像加了盐一样有分寸（意指言谈有味且恰当）。努力为每个人找到最合适的话语。♡ Lara

> Hello Siyuan!
 
I`m happy that you liked the stamp, but I`m sorry that I don`t remember which one you got.
I know that I try to use special turist stamps. These are with typical norwegian motives (Nature, northern ligths or buildings)
 
If you are really interested in finding out, you may send me a picture of the stamp and I will try to answer your question a little better this time.
 
Have a nice day
Dani

* 翻译：

我很高兴你喜欢这枚邮票，但我很抱歉我不记得你得到的是哪一枚。

如果你真的有兴趣了解更多，可以给我发送这枚邮票的照片，我会尽量更好地回答你的问题。
祝你有美好的一天！
丹尼

[NL-2169514](https://www.postcrossing.com/postcards/NL-2169514)

> 来自 [Tammy76](https://www.postcrossing.com/user/Tammy76) 🇳🇱
> 📤 [Netherlands](https://www.bing.com/maps/?cp=50.88327~5.92978&lvl=12.0&setlang=zh-Hans) 2013/11/06 13:03 (当地)
> 📥 [China](https://www.bing.com/maps/?cp=29.82739~106.43645&lvl=12.0&setlang=zh-Hans) 2013/12/09 19:25 (当地)
 📏 8,173 | ⏱ 33

:::tabs
@tab 图片
<div class="image-preview">  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/gallery/picture/" />  <img src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator@main/template/content/NL-2169514.webp" /></div>

@tab 内容
* 卡片文字

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 识别]`
Hello Siyuan,
I'm writing you from my town Voerendaal, in the south of The Netherlands. It has a population of +/- 12,500 people.
It is very chilly here. At the moment 3°C (12:4 hour). Since this week the frost set in at night. Brrr...
We are getting ready to celebrate Sinterklaas (Saint Nicholas) on December 5. It is a fest for children, unfortunately it was on international news because some people think that his happy helpers Zwarte Pieten (Black Petes) are racism. Believe me, anyone who celebrate this fest for children doesn't agree to that. Maybe you heard something about it.
My daughter (3) likes Sinterklaas (Saint Nicholas) and the Zwarte Pieten (Black Petes) very much. It is a beautiful tradition where we lie to kids the same as we do about Santa Claus! 😊
Groetjes (Greetings) Tamara

* 翻译：

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 翻译]`
你好冯思远，
我正从荷兰南部的小镇福伦达尔（Voerendaal）给你写信。这里大约有一万两千五百名居民。
这里天气非常冷，目前是摄氏 3 度。从这周开始，夜里已经结霜了。冷得发抖……
我们正准备庆祝 12 月 5 日的圣尼古拉斯节（Sinterklaas）。这是一个属于孩子们的节日，遗憾的是它上了国际新闻，因为有些人认为他那些快乐的帮手“黑彼得”（Zwarte Pieten）带有种族主义色彩。相信我，任何为孩子们庆祝这个节日的人都不会同意这种说法。也许你听说过这件事。
我三岁的女儿非常喜欢圣尼古拉斯和“黑彼得”。这是一个美丽的传统，我们像对待圣诞老人一样对孩子们编织着美丽的谎言！😊
Groetjes（问候）Tamara


:::

> `[由imap_tools提取]`
“Hello Arthur,
thank you so much for your great card  and the nice stamps of the year of the rabbit, snake dragon.  🤩
Your bike trip sounds very interesting. 
And now I have to say I'm so sorry for my late registration if you card. I have mental health issues for month and it was a big fight. I didn't have a lot of energy and strengt doing a lot and I was stressed a lot, so that I have to cancel a lot of nice things. Things I thought they bring my joy changed into a burden and exhausting me. And I have little children so I had to be there for them. I thought sometimes now I'm in the right mood and than get a flashback to my bad time within hours or within one or two days. It was so crazy. In my good times I wrote cards and thought "Wow now I'm back." No I wasn't. It was only a fake. And my family than decided to take all my postage which is coming and hide it for me until I'm better and now is the time, so they give my all my postage and it was overwhelming. In a good way, but also in a bad, because I know that there are lovely people waiting for my replay and registration. I hope you can forgive me, even if it's just hard. 
I'm wishing you all the best and may the sun always shine for you.
Lovely greetings,
Sandra”

* 翻译：

> `[由Gemini gemini-3.1-flash-lite-preview 翻译]`
你好 Arthur，
非常感谢你寄来的精美明信片，以及兔年、蛇年和龙年的漂亮邮票。🤩
你的骑行之旅听起来非常有趣。
现在，我必须为我迟迟没有登记你的明信片向你道歉。过去几个月我一直受心理健康问题的困扰，那是一场艰难的战斗。我没有足够的精力和力量去做很多事情，压力也非常大，以至于不得不取消了许多美好的计划。那些我原以为会给我带来快乐的事情，却变成了沉重的负担，让我精疲力竭。况且我还有年幼的孩子需要照顾，我必须陪伴在他们身边。有时我以为自己调整好了状态，可几个小时或一两天后，糟糕的回忆又会涌上心头。这真的很折磨人。在状态好一点的时候，我写了一些明信片，心里想着“哇，我终于好起来了”。但其实并不是，那只是假象。后来我的家人决定把所有寄给我的邮件都收起来，帮我保管直到我好转。现在时机到了，他们把所有的邮件都交给了我，这让我感到有些不知所措。这种感觉既美好又沉重，因为我知道有许多可爱的人在等待我的回复和登记。希望你能原谅我，尽管这确实很难。
祝你一切顺利，愿阳光永远照耀着你。
诚挚的问候，
Sandra

来自 Burgwedel 的 Antonia 🙋🏼‍♀️

:::
